--下位互換テーブル
drop table if exists spec.cvo;
create table spec.cvo as select superior, crop, family, synonym, kana, nomen, english,  harvest, cultivate, use, maturity, concat('|', heading, note) as note, sakumotsu, itgl, bunruihyo, seibunhyo, wamei, hinshu, ncbi, wikipedia, agrovoc from spec.cvo2;
